 Nepali Congress President Sushil Koirala was elected the new Prime Minister of Nepal on Monday
 nepali samvidhansabha main 575 maton main se do tihaai mat hasil kar koirala nepal ke 37wein pradhanmantri bane
 The President of the Constituent Assembly Surya Bahadur Thapa declared Koirala to get 405 votes
 ekikrut nepal communist party (maovadi) or kuch seemaant partiyon ke 148 sansad sadasyon ne koirala ke virodh main matdaan kiya
 However, 74-year-old Koirala was the only candidate for the post of Nepalese Prime Minister, with the support of several political parties, including the Unified Nepal Communist Party (marxist-leninist)
 koirala nepal ke mukhya nyaayadhish khil raaj regmi kii adhyakshata vaali antarim sarkaar kii jagah nepal kii satta sanbhaalenge
 Of the 30 political parties representing the Constituent Assembly of Nepal, 16 parties voted against Koirala, although they won a majority based on the number of members
 pehali samvidhansabha ke khandit hone ke 21 maheene baad tathaa duusari samvidhansabha ke chune jane ke teen maheene baad nepal main chuni hui nai sarkaar bani
 The newly elected Prime Minister made his first address to the House and assured to bring the federal democratic constitution within a year
 iske alaava unhone samast sansadhano kaa upyog nepal ke aarthik vikaas ke liye kiye jane kaa aashwaasan bhi diya
 He is the fourth member of the Koirala family to become the Prime Minister of Koiralanepal, a famous political house and associated with Nepal's democratic struggle
 unase pehle maatrakaa prasad koirala (1951-52 or 1953-55), bisheshwar prasad koirala (1959-60) or girija prasad koirala (1991-94, 1998-99, 2001-01 tathaa 2007-08) nepal ke pradhanmantri rah chuke hai
 Sushil Koirala, however, has not held any position till now in his political career
 nepali congress ke samarpit sadsy rahe koirala 1974 main vimaan apharan cond main sanliptata ke chalate bharat main teen varsh ke liye jail kii sajaa bhi kaat chuke hai

 nepal ke divangat maharaj mahendra dwaara party viheen panchayat pranali lagu karne or loktantr ke liye ladane vaale anek netaaon ko jail main daal die jane ke baad 1960 main koirala nepal se kolkata chale gaye
 In Kolkata, he met the then Chief Minister of West Bengal, Bidham Chandra Roy, to seek moral support for the ongoing struggle for democracy in Nepal

 Koirala, while living in exile, edited the Nepali Congress official letter 'tarun'
 koirala 1979 se nepali congress kii kendriya kaaryakarini ke sadsy rahe, tathaa 1996 main mahasachiv or 1998 main upaadhyaksh chune gaye
 Koirala was appointed acting president of the Nepali Congress in 2008 by the then president Girija Prasad Koirala, and in 2010 he was elected the party's president
 centre sarkaar main shaamil diemke ke sabhi 6 mantri somvaar ko apana istipha saunp denge

 kangra kaa brajareshwari shaktipeeth maa kaa chamatkaari dham he
 One of the 52 Shaktipeeths fell right in the Brajreshwari Shaktipeeth
 yahaan 3 dharmon ke pratik ke rup main maa kii 3 pindion kii puja hoti he
 It is said that when Mother Sati was angry with the insult of Shiva committed by her father and sacrificed her life by jumping into the sacrificial fire of her father King Daksha, the angry Shiva roamed the whole creation with his body
 shiv kaa krodh shant karne ke liye bhagwaan vishnu ne apane chakra se mata sati ke sharir ke tukade-tukade kar die
 These places of the body where they fell on the earth are called Shaktipeeth
 manyata he ki yahaan mata sati kaa dahinaa vaksh gira tha isliye brajareshwari shaktipeeth main maa ke vaksh kii puja hoti he
 This Shaktipeeth of Mata Brajeshwari is unique and special in itself because here not only Hindu devotees bow down the head but also devotees of Muslim and Sikh religion come to this temple and offer flowers of their faith
 kehete hai bajreshwari devi mandir ke 3 gumbad in 3 dharmon ke pratik hai pehla hindu dharm kaa pratik he jisaki akruti mandir jaisi he to doosraa muslim samaaj kaa or teesraa gumbad sikh sampradaay kaa pratik he
 Mother damsels are also three in this abode of mother with 3 domes and called the center of faith of 3 sects
 mandir ke garbhagrih main pratishthit ye pehali or mukhya pindi maa brajareshwari kii he
 The second mother is of Bhadrakali and the third and the youngest Pindi mother is Ekadashi
 maa ke is shaktipeeth main hi unke param bhakt dhyanu ne apana sheesh arpit kiya tha
 Therefore, the devotees of the mother who are also followers of Dhyanu, wear yellow clothes and come to the temple and worship themselves, and bless themselves
 kehete hai jo bhi bhakt man main sachhee shraddha lekar maa ke is darbar main pahunchataa he uski koi bhi manokamana adhuri nahin rahati
 Then whether it is the wish of the life partner, or the desire to have children
 maa apane har bhakt kii muraad puri karti hai
 In this court of the mother there is a law of aarti 5 times, which every devotee desires to witness
 savere mandir ke dwaar khulte hi bhakt aatur ho jate hai maa ke darshan pujan ko
 The puja that fulfills every wish of theirs and all their troubles are removed
 maa brajeshwari devi kii is shaktipeeth main pratidin maa kii 5 baar aarti hoti he
 The bed of the mother is first raised as soon as the doors of the temple are opened in the morning
 uske baad raatri ke shringaar main hi maa kii mangala aarti kii jaati he
 After Mangala Aarti, the mother's nightly makeup is taken off and her three pindi are anointed with water, milk, curd, ghee and honey
 uske baad pile chandan se maa kaa shringaar kar unhen nae vastra or sone ke aabhushan pahanaaen jate hai
 Then the morning aarti of the mother is done by offering gram, puri and fruits
 dopaher kii aarti or bhoga chadhaane kii rasm ko gupt rakhaa jaataa he
 The temple doors are closed for the midday Arti, when the devotees get their children shaved at a special place built in the temple premises itself
 manyata he ki yahaan bacchon kaa mundan karwaane se maa bacchon ke jivan kii samast aapadaaon ko har leti hai
 There is also a temple of Lord Bhairav in the temple premises, but women are totally forbidden to visit this temple
 yahaan viraaje bhagwaan bhairav kii murti badi hi khaas he kehete hai jab bhi kangra par koi musiibat aane vaali hoti he to is murti kii ankhon se aansu or sharir se pasinaa nikalne lagata he
 Then the priest of the temple organizes a huge havan and requests the mother to avoid the disaster and this is the miracle and glory of Brajeshwari Shaktipeeth, every disaster is averted with the blessing of the mother
 dopaher baad mandir ke kapaat dobaaraa bhakton ke liye khol die jate hai or bhakt maa kaa aashirwad lene pahunch jate hai
 It is said that rice is not used on Ekadashi, but Mother Ekadashi itself is present in this Shaktipeeth, so rice is offered here as a bhog
 suryaast ke baad in pindion ko snaan karakar panchamrita se inkaa dobaaraa abhishek kiya jaataa he
 The mother is adorned by wearing red sandalwood, flowers and new clothes and concludes the evening with the evening
 shaam kii aarti kaa bhoga bhakton main prasad rup main baanta jaataa he
 Time comes at night for mother's sleeping aarti, when the temple priest prepares the mother's bed and worships the mother
 dilli ke sangam vihaar ilaake main ek yuvak ko doston ke saamne apni pistal chamakaana baari pad gaya

 use dost aspataal lekar gaye, lekin bachaane kii kai koshishon ke baavjood uski maut ho gai

 vahaan bablu or amit ne bear pi

 amit ne pistal ko shart ke andar rakhaa tha

 is par amit ne kaha kii ye usne khud kii suraksha ke liye le rakhi he or ye kah kar usne pistal kii magazine nikaali or pistal ko apane sir par rakhkar bolaa kii dekho kuch nahin he
 Rajneesh and Bablu told the police that both were trying to stop him during this time but by then he opened fire and a bullet inside the pistol went straight into his head
 iske baad bablu or rajnish donon amit ko lekar hospital gaye
 Police have registered a case of culpable homicide and Arms Act in this case and are investigating
 police bablu or rajnish ke bayaan kii jaanch kar rahi he
 Important changes have been made in the names of several schemes of the Union Government's third budget presented recently
 bajet main sarkaar ne purv pradhanmantri rajeev gandhi ke naam par chal rahi chaar yojanaon ke naamon ko badal diya he

 yah naam ek april 2016 se lagu hoga
